dir=\"auto\"\u003eUse when:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eA preferred pattern exists\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSome variation is acceptable\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eConfiguration affects behavior\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExample:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"## Generate report\n\nUse this template and customize as needed:\n\n```python\ndef generate_report(data, format=\u0026quot;markdown\u0026quot;, include_charts=True):\n    # Process data\n    # Generate output in specified format\n    # Optionally include visualizations\n```\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eGenerate report\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\nUse this template and customize as needed:\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003epython\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003einclude_charts\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eTrue\u003c/span\u003e):\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Process data\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Generate output in specified format\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Optionally include visualizations\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eLow freedom\u003c/strong\u003e (specific scripts, few or no parameters):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eUse when:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eOperations are fragile and error-prone\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eConsistency is critical\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eA specific sequence must be followed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExample:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"## Database migration\n\nRun exactly this script:\n\n```bash\npython scripts/migrate.py --verify --backup\n```\n\nDo not modify the command or add additional flags.\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eDatabase migration\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\nRun exactly this script:\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003ebash\u003c/span\u003e\npython scripts/migrate.py --verify --backup\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\n\nDo not modify the command or add additional flags.\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAnalogy\u003c/strong\u003e: Think of Claude as a robot exploring a path:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNarrow bridge with cliffs on both sides\u003c/strong\u003e: There's only one safe way forward. Provide specific guardrails and exact instructions (low freedom). Example: database migrations that must run in exact sequence.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOpen field with no hazards\u003c/strong\u003e: Many paths lead to success. Give general direction and trust Claude to find the best route (high freedom). Example: code reviews where context determines the best approach.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eTest with all models you plan to use\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-test-with-all-models-you-plan-to-use\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Test with all models you plan to use\" href=\"#test-with-all-models-you-plan-to-use\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSkills act as additions to models, so effectiveness depends on the underlying model. Test your Skill with all the models you plan to use it with.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTesting considerations by model\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClaude Haiku\u003c/strong\u003e (fast, economical): Does the Skill provide enough guidance?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClaude Sonnet\u003c/strong\u003e (balanced): Is the Skill clear and efficient?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClaude Opus\u003c/strong\u003e (powerful reasoning): Does the Skill avoid over-explaining?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhat works perfectly for Opus might need more detail for Haiku. If you plan to use your Skill across multiple models, aim for instructions that work well with all of them.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eSkill structure\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-skill-structure\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Skill structure\" href=\"#skill-structure\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\n  **YAML Frontmatter**: The SKILL.md frontmatter supports two fields:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ename\u003c/code\u003e - We recommend using \u003cstrong\u003egerund form\u003c/strong\u003e (verb + -ing) for Skill names, as this clearly describes the activity or capability the Skill provides.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGood naming examples (gerund form)\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"Processing PDFs\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"Analyzing spreadsheets\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"Managing databases\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"Testing code\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"Writing documentation\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAcceptable alternatives\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eNoun phrases: \"PDF Processing\", \"Spreadsheet Analysis\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAction-oriented: \"Process PDFs\", \"Analyze Spreadsheets\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAvoid\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul to:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eReference Skills in documentation and conversations\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUnderstand what a Skill does at a 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe \u003ccode\u003edescription\u003c/code\u003e field enables Skill discovery and should include both what the Skill does and when to use it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n  **Always write in third person**. The description is injected into the system prompt, and inconsistent point-of-view can cause discovery problems.\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGood:\u003c/strong\u003e \"Processes Excel files and generates reports\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAvoid:\u003c/strong\u003e \"I can help you process Excel files\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAvoid:\u003c/strong\u003e \"You can use this to process Excel files\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBe specific and include key terms\u003c/strong\u003e. Include both what the Skill does and specific triggers/contexts for when to use it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEach Skill has exactly one description field. The description is critical for skill selection: Claude uses it to choose the right Skill from potentially 100+ available Skills. Your description must provide enough detail for Claude to know when to select this Skill, while the rest of SKILL.md provides the implementation details.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEffective examples:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePDF Processing skill:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"description: Extract text and tables from PDF files, fill forms, merge documents. Use when working with PDF files or when the user mentions PDFs, forms, or document extraction.\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003edescription\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eExtract text and tables from PDF files, fill forms, merge documents. Use when the user asks for help writing commit messages or reviewing staged changes.\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003edescription\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003eGenerate descriptive commit messages by analyzing git diffs. of contents in an onboarding guide. to organize instructions, code, and resources effectively\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch4 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eUse workflows for complex tasks\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-use-workflows-for-complex-tasks\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Use workflows for complex tasks\" 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBreak complex operations into clear, sequential steps. For particularly complex workflows, provide a checklist that Claude can copy into its response and check off as it progresses.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExample 1: Research synthesis workflow\u003c/strong\u003e (for Skills without code):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"## Research synthesis workflow\n\nCopy this checklist and track your progress:\n\n```\nResearch Progress:\n- [ ] Step 1: Read all source documents\n- [ ] Step 2: Identify key themes\n- [ ] Step 3: Cross-reference claims\n- [ ] Step 4: Create structured summary\n- [ ] Step 5: Verify citations\n```\n\n**Step 1: Read all source documents**\n\nReview each document in the `sources/` directory. Note the main arguments and supporting evidence.\n\n**Step 2: Identify key themes**\n\nLook for patterns across sources. What themes appear repeatedly? Where do sources agree or disagree?\n\n**Step 3: Cross-reference claims**\n\nFor each major claim, verify it appears in the source material. Note which source supports each point.\n\n**Step 4: Create structured summary**\n\nOrganize findings by theme. Include:\n- Main claim\n- Supporting evidence from sources\n- Conflicting viewpoints (if any)\n\n**Step 5: Verify citations**\n\nCheck that every claim references the correct source document. If citations are incomplete, return to Step 3.\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eResearch synthesis workflow\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\nCopy this checklist and track your progress:\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eResearch Progress:\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 1: Read all source documents\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 2: Identify key themes\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 3: Cross-reference claims\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 4: Create structured summary\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 5: Verify citations\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 1: Read all source documents\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nReview each document in the \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003esources/\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e directory. Note the main arguments and supporting evidence.\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 2: Identify key themes\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nLook for patterns across sources. What themes appear repeatedly? Where do sources agree or disagree?\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 3: Cross-reference claims\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nFor each major claim, verify it appears in the source material. Note which source supports each point.\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 4: Create structured summary\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nOrganize findings by theme. Include:\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Main claim\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Supporting evidence from sources\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Conflicting viewpoints (if any)\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 5: Verify citations\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nCheck that every claim references the correct source document. If citations are incomplete, return to Step 3.\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis example shows how workflows apply to analysis tasks that don't require code. The checklist pattern works for any complex, multi-step process.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExample 2: PDF form filling workflow\u003c/strong\u003e (for Skills with code):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"## PDF form filling workflow\n\nCopy this checklist and check off items as you complete them:\n\n```\nTask Progress:\n- [ ] Step 1: Analyze the form (run analyze_form.py)\n- [ ] Step 2: Create field mapping (edit fields.json)\n- [ ] Step 3: Validate mapping (run validate_fields.py)\n- [ ] Step 4: Fill the form (run fill_form.py)\n- [ ] Step 5: Verify output (run verify_output.py)\n```\n\n**Step 1: Analyze the form**\n\nRun: `python scripts/analyze_form.py input.pdf`\n\nThis extracts form fields and their locations, saving to `fields.json`.\n\n**Step 2: Create field mapping**\n\nEdit `fields.json` to add values for each field.\n\n**Step 3: Validate mapping**\n\nRun: `python scripts/validate_fields.py fields.json`\n\nFix any validation errors before continuing.\n\n**Step 4: Fill the form**\n\nRun: `python scripts/fill_form.py input.pdf fields.json output.pdf`\n\n**Step 5: Verify output**\n\nRun: `python scripts/verify_output.py output.pdf`\n\nIf verification fails, return to Step 2.\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003ePDF form filling workflow\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\nCopy this checklist and check off items as you complete them:\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eTask Progress:\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 1: Analyze the form (run analyze_form.py)\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 2: Create field mapping (edit fields.json)\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 3: Validate mapping (run validate_fields.py)\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 4: Fill the form (run fill_form.py)\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e- [ ] Step 5: Verify output (run verify_output.py)\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 1: Analyze the form\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nRun: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003epython scripts/analyze_form.py input.pdf\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\n\nThis extracts form fields and their locations, saving to \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003efields.json\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e.\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 2: Create field mapping\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nEdit \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003efields.json\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e to add values for each field.\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 3: Validate mapping\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nRun: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003epython scripts/validate_fields.py fields.json\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\n\nFix any validation errors before continuing.\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 4: Fill the form\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nRun: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003epython scripts/fill_form.py input.pdf fields.json output.pdf\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eStep 5: Verify output\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\n\nRun: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003epython scripts/verify_output.py output.pdf\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e`\u003c/span\u003e\n\nIf verification fails, return to Step 2.\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eClear steps prevent Claude from skipping critical validation. data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"## Report structure\n\nHere is a sensible default format, but use your best judgment based on the analysis:\n\n```markdown\n# [Analysis Title]\n\n## Executive summary\n[Overview]\n\n## Key findings\n[Adapt sections based on what you discover]\n\n## Recommendations\n[Tailor to the specific context]\n```\n\nAdjust sections as needed for the specific analysis type.\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eReport structure\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\nHere is a sensible default format, but use your best judgment based on the analysis:\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003emarkdown\u003c/span\u003e\n# [Analysis Title]\n\n## Executive summary\n[Overview]\n\n## Key findings\n[Adapt sections based on what you discover]\n\n## Recommendations\n[Tailor to the specific context]\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\n\nAdjust sections as needed for the specific analysis type.\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor Skills where output quality depends on seeing examples, provide input/output pairs just like in regular prompting:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"## Commit message format\n\nGenerate commit messages following these examples:\n\n**Example 1:**\nInput: Added user authentication with JWT tokens\nOutput:\n```\nfeat(auth): implement JWT-based authentication\n\nAdd login endpoint and token validation middleware\n```\n\n**Example 2:**\nInput: Fixed bug where dates displayed incorrectly in reports\nOutput:\n```\nfix(reports): correct date formatting in timezone conversion\n\nUse UTC timestamps consistently across report generation\n```\n\n**Example 3:**\nInput: Updated dependencies and refactored error handling\nOutput:\n```\nchore: update dependencies and refactor error handling\n\n- Upgrade lodash to 4.17.21\n- Standardize error response format across endpoints\n```\n\nFollow this style: type(scope): brief description, then detailed explanation.\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eCommit message format\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\nGenerate commit messages following these examples:\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eExample 1:\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\nInput: Added user authentication with JWT tokens\nOutput:\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003efeat(auth): implement JWT-based authentication\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan 3:\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e\nInput: Updated dependencies and refactored error handling\nOutput:\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan endpoints\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\n\nFollow this style: type(scope): brief description, then detailed explanation.\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eExamples help Claude understand the desired style and level of detail more clearly than descriptions alone.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eConditional workflow pattern\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca points:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"## Document modification workflow\n\n1. Determine the modification type:\n\n   **Creating new content?**  Follow \u0026quot;Creation workflow\u0026quot; below\n   **Editing existing content?**  Follow \u0026quot;Editing workflow\u0026quot; below\n\n2. Creation workflow:\n   - Use docx-js library\n   - Build document from scratch\n   - Export to .docx format\n\n3. Editing workflow:\n   - Unpack existing document\n   - Modify XML directly\n   - Validate after each change\n   - Repack when complete\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eDocument modification workflow\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e1\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e Determine the modification type:\n\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eCreating new content?\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e  Follow \"Creation workflow\" below\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003eEditing existing content?\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e**\u003c/span\u003e  Follow \"Editing workflow\" below\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e2\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e Creation workflow:\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Use docx-js library\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Build document from scratch\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Export to .docx format\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e3\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e Editing workflow:\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Unpack existing document\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Modify XML directly\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Validate after each change\n   \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e Repack when complete\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\n  If workflows become large or complicated with many steps, consider pushing them into separate files and tell Claude to read the appropriate file based on the task at hand.\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eEvaluation and iteration\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-evaluation-and-iteration\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Evaluation and iteration\" href=\"#evaluation-and-iteration\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eBuild evaluations first\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-build-evaluations-first\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Build evaluations first\" href=\"#build-evaluations-first\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCreate evaluations BEFORE writing extensive documentation.\u003c/strong\u003e This ensures your Skill solves real problems rather than documenting imagined ones.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEvaluation-driven development:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIdentify gaps\u003c/strong\u003e: Run Claude on representative tasks without a Skill. Document specific failures or missing context\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCreate evaluations\u003c/strong\u003e: Build three scenarios that test these gaps\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEstablish baseline\u003c/strong\u003e: Measure Claude's performance without the Skill\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWrite minimal instructions\u003c/strong\u003e: Create just enough content to address the gaps and pass evaluations\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIterate\u003c/strong\u003e: Execute evaluations, compare against baseline, and refine\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis approach ensures you're solving actual problems rather than anticipating requirements that may never materialize.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eEvaluation structure\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"{\n  \u0026quot;skills\u0026quot;: [\u0026quot;pdf-processing\u0026quot;],\n  \u0026quot;query\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;Extract all text from this PDF file and save it to output.txt\u0026quot;,\n  \u0026quot;files\u0026quot;: [\u0026quot;test-files/document.pdf\u0026quot;],\n  \u0026quot;expected_behavior\u0026quot;: [\n    \u0026quot;Successfully reads the PDF file using an appropriate PDF processing library or command-line tool\u0026quot;,\n    \u0026quot;Extracts text content from all pages in the document without missing any pages\u0026quot;,\n    \u0026quot;Saves the extracted text to a file named output.txt in a clear, readable format\u0026quot;\n  ]\n}\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e{\n  \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"skills\"\u003c/span\u003e: [\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003epdf-processing\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e],\n  \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"query\"\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eExtract all text from this PDF file and save it to output.txt\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,\n  \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"files\"\u003c/span\u003e: [\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003etest-files/document.pdf\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e],\n  \u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003e\"expected_behavior\"\u003c/span\u003e: [\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eSuccessfully reads the PDF file using an appropriate PDF processing library or command-line tool\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eExtracts text content from all pages in the document without missing any pages\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e,\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003eSaves the extracted text to a file named output.txt in a clear, readable format\u003cspan class=\"pl-pds\"\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\n  ]\n}\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\n  This example demonstrates a data-driven evaluation with a simple testing rubric. We do not currently provide a built-in way to run these evaluations. Users can create their own evaluation system. Evaluations are your source of truth for measuring Skill effectiveness.\n\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eDevelop Skills iteratively with Claude\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-develop-skills-iteratively-with-claude\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Develop Skills iteratively with Claude\" href=\"#develop-skills-iteratively-with-claude\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe most effective Skill development process involves Claude itself. Work with one instance of Claude (\"Claude A\") to create a Skill that will be used by other instances (\"Claude B\"). Claude A helps you design and refine instructions, while Claude B tests them in real tasks. This works because Claude models understand both how to write effective agent instructions and what information agents need.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCreating a new Skill:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eComplete a task without a Skill\u003c/strong\u003e: Work through a problem with Claude A using normal prompting. As you work, you'll naturally provide context, explain preferences, and share procedural knowledge. Notice what information you repeatedly provide.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIdentify the reusable pattern\u003c/strong\u003e: After completing the task, identify what context you provided that would be useful for similar future tasks.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExample\u003c/strong\u003e: If you worked through a BigQuery analysis, you might have provided table names, field definitions, filtering rules (like \"always exclude test accounts\"), and common query patterns.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAsk Claude A to create a Skill\u003c/strong\u003e: \"Create a Skill that captures this BigQuery analysis pattern we just used. Include the table schemas, naming conventions, and the rule about filtering test accounts.\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\n  Claude models understand the Skill format and structure natively. You don't need special system prompts or a \"writing skills\" skill to get Claude to help create Skills. Simply ask Claude to create a Skill and it will generate properly structured SKILL.md content with appropriate frontmatter and body content.\n\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReview for conciseness\u003c/strong\u003e: Check that Claude A hasn't added unnecessary explanations. Ask: \"Remove the explanation about what win rate means - Claude already knows that.\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImprove information architecture\u003c/strong\u003e: Ask Claude A to organize the content more effectively. For example: \"Organize this so the table schema is in a separate reference file. We might add more tables later.\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTest on similar tasks\u003c/strong\u003e: Use the Skill with Claude B (a fresh instance with the Skill loaded) on related use cases. Observe whether Claude B finds the right information, applies rules correctly, and handles the task successfully.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIterate based on observation\u003c/strong\u003e: If Claude B struggles or misses something, return to Claude A with specifics: \"When Claude used this Skill, it forgot to filter by date for Q4. Should we add a section about date filtering patterns?\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIterating on existing Skills:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe same hierarchical pattern continues when improving Skills. You alternate between:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWorking with Claude A\u003c/strong\u003e (the expert who helps refine the Skill)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTesting with Claude B\u003c/strong\u003e (the agent using the Skill to perform real work)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObserving Claude B's behavior\u003c/strong\u003e and bringing insights back to Claude A\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUse the Skill in real workflows\u003c/strong\u003e: Give Claude B (with the Skill loaded) actual tasks, not test scenarios\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eObserve Claude B's behavior\u003c/strong\u003e: Note where it struggles, succeeds, or makes unexpected choices\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExample observation\u003c/strong\u003e: \"When I asked Claude B for a regional sales report, it wrote the query but forgot to filter out test accounts, even though the Skill mentions this rule.\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReturn to Claude A for improvements\u003c/strong\u003e: Share the current SKILL.md and describe what you observed. Ask: \"I noticed Claude B forgot to filter test accounts when I asked for a regional report. The Skill mentions filtering, but maybe it's not prominent enough?\"\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReview Claude A's suggestions\u003c/strong\u003e: Claude A might suggest reorganizing to make rules more prominent, using stronger language like \"MUST filter\" instead of \"always filter\", or restructuring the workflow section.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eApply and test changes\u003c/strong\u003e: Update the Skill with Claude A's refinements, then test again with Claude B on similar requests\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRepeat based on usage\u003c/strong\u003e: Continue this observe-refine-test cycle as you encounter new scenarios. Each iteration improves the Skill based on real agent behavior, not assumptions.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGathering team feedback:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eShare Skills with teammates and observe their usage\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAsk: Does the Skill activate when expected? Are instructions clear? What's missing?\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIncorporate feedback to address blind spots in your own usage patterns\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhy this approach works\u003c/strong\u003e: Claude A understands agent needs, you provide domain expertise, Claude B reveals gaps through real usage, and iterative refinement improves Skills based on observed behavior rather than assumptions.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eObserve how Claude navigates Skills\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-observe-how-claude-navigates-skills\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Observe how Claude navigates Skills\" href=\"#observe-how-claude-navigates-skills\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAs you iterate on Skills, pay attention to how Claude actually uses them in practice. Watch for:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eUnexpected exploration paths\u003c/strong\u003e: Does Claude read files in an order you didn't anticipate? This might indicate your structure isn't as intuitive as you thought\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMissed connections\u003c/strong\u003e: Does Claude fail to follow references to important files? Your links might need to be more explicit or prominent\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOverreliance on certain sections\u003c/strong\u003e: If Claude repeatedly reads the same file, consider whether that content should be in the main SKILL.md instead\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eIgnored content\u003c/strong\u003e: If Claude never accesses a bundled file, it might be unnecessary or poorly signaled in the main instructions\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIterate based on these observations rather than assumptions. The 'name' and 'description' in your Skill's metadata are particularly critical. Claude uses these when deciding whether to trigger the Skill in response to the current task. Make sure they clearly describe what the Skill does and when it should be used.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" Windows:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e \u003cstrong\u003eGood\u003c/strong\u003e: \u003ccode\u003escripts/helper.py\u003c/code\u003e, Unix systems.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eAvoid offering too many pdfplumber, or PyMuPDF, or pdf2image, or...\u0026quot;\n\n**Good example: Provide a default** (with escape hatch):\n\u0026quot;Use pdfplumber for text extraction:\n```python\nimport If your Skill uses only markdown instructions, skip to \u003ca href=\"#checklist-for-effective-skills\"\u003eChecklist for effective Skills\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eSolve, don't punt\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-solve-dont-punt\" 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen writing scripts for Skills, handle error conditions rather than punting to Claude.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGood example: Handle errors explicitly\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def process_file(path):\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Process a file, creating it if it doesn't exist.\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    try:\n        with open(path) as f:\n            return f.read()\n    except FileNotFoundError:\n        # Create file with default content instead of failing\n        print(f\u0026quot;File {path} not found, creating default\u0026quot;)\n        with open(path, 'w') as f:\n            f.write('')\n        return ''\n    except PermissionError:\n        # Provide alternative instead of failing\n        print(f\u0026quot;Cannot access {path}, using default\u0026quot;)\n        return ''\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ereturn\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e''\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBad example: Punt to Claude\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def process_file(path):\n    # Just fail and let Claude figure it out\n    return open(path).read()\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eprocess_file\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003epath\u003c/span\u003e):\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Just fail and let Claude figure it out\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003ereturn\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eopen\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003epath\u003c/span\u003e).\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eread\u003c/span\u003e()\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eConfiguration parameters should also be justified and documented to avoid \"voodoo constants\" (Ousterhout's law). If you don't know the right value, how will Claude determine it?\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGood example: Self-documenting\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# HTTP requests typically complete within 30 seconds\n# Longer timeout accounts for slow connections\nREQUEST_TIMEOUT = 30\n\n# Three retries balances reliability vs speed\n# Most intermittent failures resolve by the second retry\nMAX_RETRIES = 3\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# HTTP requests typically complete within 30 seconds\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e# Longer timeout accounts for slow dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBenefits of utility scripts\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eMore reliable than generated alt=\"Bundling executable scripts alongside instruction files\" width=\"2000\" height=\"1154\" data-canonical-src=\"https://mintcdn.com/anthropic-claude-docs/4Bny2bjzuGBK7o00/images/agent-skills-executable-scripts.png?fit=max\u0026amp;auto=format\u0026amp;n=4Bny2bjzuGBK7o00\u0026amp;q=85\u0026amp;s=4bbc45f2c2e0bee9f2f0d5da669bad00\" style=\"max-width: 100%; height: auto; max-height: 1154px;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe diagram above shows how executable scripts work alongside instruction files. The instruction file (forms.md) references the script, and Claude can execute it without loading its contents into context.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImportant distinction\u003c/strong\u003e: Make clear in your instructions whether Claude should:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExecute the script\u003c/strong\u003e (most common): \"Run \u003ccode\u003eanalyze_form.py\u003c/code\u003e to extract fields\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eRead it as reference\u003c/strong\u003e (for complex logic): \"See \u003ccode\u003eanalyze_form.py\u003c/code\u003e for the field extraction algorithm\"\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor most utility scripts, execution is preferred because it's more reliable and efficient. See the \u003ca href=\"#runtime-environment\"\u003eRuntime environment\u003c/a\u003e section below for details on how script execution works.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExample\u003c/strong\u003e:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"## Utility scripts\n\n**analyze_form.py**: Extract all form fields from PDF\n\n```bash\npython scripts/analyze_form.py input.pdf \u0026gt; fields.json\n```\n\nOutput format:\n```json\n{\n  \u0026quot;field_name\u0026quot;: {\u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;text\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;x\u0026quot;: 100, \u0026quot;y\u0026quot;: 200},\n  \u0026quot;signature\u0026quot;: {\u0026quot;type\u0026quot;: \u0026quot;sig\u0026quot;, \u0026quot;x\u0026quot;: 150, \u0026quot;y\u0026quot;: 500}\n}\n```\n\n**validate_boxes.py**: Check for overlapping bounding boxes\n\n```bash\npython scripts/validate_boxes.py fields.json\n# Returns: \u0026quot;OK\u0026quot; or lists conflicts\n```\n\n**fill_form.py**: Apply field values to PDF\n\n```bash\npython scripts/fill_form.py input.pdf fields.json output.pdf\n```\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-mh\"\u003e## \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eUtility class=\"pl-k\"\u003e\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e fields.json\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\n\nOutput format:\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e```\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen Claude performs complex, open-ended tasks, it can make mistakes. The \"plan-validate-execute\" pattern catches errors early by having Claude first create a plan in a structured format, then validate that plan with a script before executing it.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExample\u003c/strong\u003e: Imagine asking Claude to update 50 form fields in a PDF based on a spreadsheet. Without validation, Claude might reference non-existent fields, create conflicting values, miss required fields, or apply updates incorrectly.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eSolution\u003c/strong\u003e: Use the workflow pattern shown above (PDF form filling), but add an intermediate \u003ccode\u003echanges.json\u003c/code\u003e file that gets validated before applying changes. The workflow becomes: analyze  \u003cstrong\u003ecreate plan file\u003c/strong\u003e  \u003cstrong\u003evalidate plan\u003c/strong\u003e  execute  verify.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhy this pattern works:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eCatches errors early\u003c/strong\u003e: Validation finds problems before changes are applied\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMachine-verifiable\u003c/strong\u003e: Scripts provide objective verification\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eReversible planning\u003c/strong\u003e: Claude can iterate on the plan without touching originals\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eClear debugging\u003c/strong\u003e: Error messages point to specific problems\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhen to use\u003c/strong\u003e: Batch operations, destructive changes, complex validation rules, high-stakes operations.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eImplementation tip\u003c/strong\u003e: Make validation scripts verbose with specific error messages like \"Field 'signature_date' not found. Available fields: customer_name, order_total, signature_date_signed\" to help Claude fix issues.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003ePackage dependencies\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-package-dependencies\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Package dependencies\" .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSkills run in the code execution environment with platform-specific limitations:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eclaude.ai\u003c/strong\u003e: Can install packages from npm and PyPI and pull from GitHub repositories\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAnthropic API\u003c/strong\u003e: Has no network access and no runtime package installation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eList required packages in your SKILL.md and verify they're available in the \u003ca href=\"/obra/superpowers/blob/main/en/docs/agents-and-tools/tool-use/code-execution-tool\"\u003ecode execution tool documentation\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eRuntime environment\u003c/h3\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-runtime-environment\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Runtime environment\" href=\"#runtime-environment\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eSkills run in a code execution environment with filesystem access, bash commands, and code execution capabilities. For the conceptual explanation of this architecture, see \u003ca href=\"/obra/superpowers/blob/main/en/docs/agents-and-tools/agent-skills/overview#the-skills-architecture\"\u003eThe Skills architecture\u003c/a\u003e in the overview.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHow this affects your authoring:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHow Claude accesses Skills:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMetadata pre-loaded\u003c/strong\u003e: At startup, the name and description from all Skills' YAML frontmatter are loaded into the system prompt\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFiles read on-demand\u003c/strong\u003e: Claude uses bash Read tools to access SKILL.md and other files from the filesystem when needed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eScripts executed efficiently\u003c/strong\u003e: Utility scripts can be executed via bash without loading their full contents into context. Only the script's output consumes tokens\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNo context penalty for large files\u003c/strong\u003e: Reference files, data, or documentation don't consume context tokens until actually read\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFile paths matter\u003c/strong\u003e: Claude navigates your skill directory like a filesystem. Use forward slashes (\u003ccode\u003ereference/guide.md\u003c/code\u003e), not backslashes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eName files descriptively\u003c/strong\u003e: Use names that indicate content: \u003ccode\u003eform_validation_rules.md\u003c/code\u003e, not \u003ccode\u003edoc2.md\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOrganize for discovery\u003c/strong\u003e: Structure directories by domain or feature\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eGood: \u003ccode\u003ereference/finance.md\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ereference/sales.md\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBad: \u003ccode\u003edocs/file1.md\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003edocs/file2.md\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eBundle comprehensive resources\u003c/strong\u003e: Include complete API docs, extensive examples, large datasets; no context penalty until accessed\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003ePrefer scripts for deterministic operations\u003c/strong\u003e: Write \u003ccode\u003evalidate_form.py\u003c/code\u003e rather than asking Claude to generate validation code\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMake execution intent clear\u003c/strong\u003e:\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"Run \u003ccode\u003eanalyze_form.py\u003c/code\u003e to extract fields\" (execute)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\"See \u003ccode\u003eanalyze_form.py\u003c/code\u003e for the extraction algorithm\" (read as reference)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTest file access patterns\u003c/strong\u003e: Verify Claude can navigate your directory structure by testing with real requests\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eExample:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"bigquery-skill/\n SKILL.md (overview, points to reference files)\n reference/\n     finance.md (revenue metrics)\n     sales.md (pipeline data)\n     product.md (usage analytics)\"\u003e\u003cpre class=\"notranslate\"\u003e\u003ccode\u003ebigquery-skill/\n SKILL.md (overview, points to reference files)\n reference/\n     finance.md (revenue metrics)\n     sales.md (pipeline data)\n     product.md (usage analytics)\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen the user asks about revenue, Claude reads SKILL.md, sees the reference to \u003ccode\u003ereference/finance.md\u003c/code\u003e, and invokes bash to read just that file. The sales.md and product.md files remain on the filesystem, consuming zero context tokens until needed. This filesystem-based model is what enables progressive disclosure. Claude can navigate and selectively load exactly what each task requires.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor complete details on the technical architecture, see \u003ca
